PolicyQuotaController struct {\n\tlogger                logrus.FieldLogger\n\tciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]\n\tmaxPerNamespace       int\n\n\t// mu protects NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tlogger logrus.FieldLogger,\n\tciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\tif logger == server\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// onUpsert handles upsert events for CiliumNetworkPolicy resources.\nfunc (c NewPolicyQuotaController(logger, mockRes, 3)\n\n\t// Initially, quota should be available\n\tassert.NoError(t, controller.CheckQuota(\"default\"))\n\n\t// Simulate adding policies\n\tpolicy1 := policy\n\tassert.NoError(t, controller.onDelete(policy1))\n\tassert.Equal(t, 2, controller.GetNamespaceCount(\"default\"))\n\n\t// Quota should be available again\n\tassert.NoError(t, controller.CheckQuota(\"default\"))\n}\n\n// TestPolicyQuotaController_MultipleNamespaces tests quota enforcement across namespaces\nfunc TestPolicyQuotaController_MultipleNamespaces(t *testing.T) namespaces\n\tpolicy1 := &cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy{\n\t\tObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{\n\t\t\tNamespace: \"ns1\",\n\t\t\tName:      \"policy1\",\n\t\t},\n\t}\n\n\tpolicy2 := &cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy{\n\t\tObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{\n\t\t\tNamespace: \"ns2\",\n\t\t\tName:      \"policy1\",\n\t\t},\n\t}\n\n\t// Add policies to different namespaces\n\tassert.NoError(t, controller.onUpsert(policy1))\n\tassert.NoError(t, controller.onUpsert(policy2))\n\n\t// Both namespaces should be independent\n\tassert.Equal(t, 1, controller.GetNamespaceCount(\"ns1\"))\n\tassert.Equal(t, 1, controller.GetNamespaceCount(\"ns2\"))\n\tassert.NoError(t, controller.CheckQuota(\"ns1\"))\n\tassert.NoError(t, controller.CheckQuota(\"ns2\"))\n\n\t// Add more policies to ns1 to exceed quota\n\tpolicy3 := &cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy{\n\t\tObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{\n\t\t\tNamespace: \"ns1\",\n\t\t\tName:      \"policy2\",\n\t\t},\n\t}\n\n\tpolicy4 := &cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy{\n\t\tObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{\n\t\t\tNamespace: \"ns1\",\n\t\t\tName:      \"policy3\",\n\t\t},\n\t}\n\n\tassert.NoError(t, controller.onUpsert(policy3))\n\tassert.NoError(t, controller.onUpsert(policy4))\n\n\t// ns1 should exceed quota\n\tassert.Equal(t, 3, controller.GetNamespaceCount(\"ns1\"))\n\tassert.Error(t, controller.CheckQuota(\"ns1\"))\n\n\t// ns2 should still have available quota\n\tassert.NoError(t, controller.CheckQuota(\"ns2\"))\n}\n\n//
